The Sārasamuccaya or ‘Essential Anthology’ by Vararuci

Digital Critical Edition of an Anthology of Sanskrit Stanzas on dharma with Old Javanese Paraphrase

edited by Arlo Griffiths

invocation

om̐ avighnam astu.

1.

1.1

bhagavān vararuci mupulakən sāra-sāra saṅ hyaṅ aṣṭādaśaparva, gave bhagavān byāsa, mataṅnyan panamaskāra sira i bhagavān byāsa, liṅnira:

Upajāti

jajñe bahujñaṁ paramābhyudāraṁ yaṁ dvīpamadhye sutam ātmabhāvāt | parāśarāt satyavatī maharṣiṁ tasmai namo ’jñānatamonudāya || 1
Parallels
  • MBh12,337.003
    jajñe bahujñaṃ param atyudāraṃ yaṃ dvīpamadhye sutam ātmavantam | parāśarād gandhavatī maharṣiṃ tasmai namo ’jñānatamonudāya ||

1.2

hana sira maharṣi, tan hana kapiṅgiṅnira, kinatvaṅan iṅ triloka, rumantasakən ptəṅniṅ ajñānaniṅ sarvabhāva, anak saṅ satyavatī, patəmvan(1) lavan bhagavān parāśara, prasūta ri tṅahnikaṅ kr̥ṣṇadvīpa, bhagavān byāsa ṅaranira, sira ta səmbahən, kamnaniṅ hulun mujarakna sāraniṅ gavenira aji.

2.

yathā samudro ’timahān yathā ca himavān giriḥ | ubhau ratnanidhī khyātau tathā bhāratam ucyate || 2
Parallels
  • MBh01,056.027 MBh18,005.052
    yathā samudro bhagavān yathā ca himavān giriḥ khyātāv ubhau ratnanidhī tathā bhāratam ucyate

2.1

nahan(2) kottamanira, kady aṅganiṅ tasik lavan gunuṅ himavān, an kalyan mās maṇik sarvamūlya, maṅkana ta sakvehnikiṅ(3) aji bhāratakathā ginavenira, an tasakan iṅ uttamarasa makādi rahasyajñāna.

3.

idaṁ kavivarair nityam ākhyānam upajīvyate | udayaprepsubhir bhr̥tyair abhijāta iveśvaraḥ || 3
Parallels
  • MBh01,002.241
    idaṃ sarvaiḥ kavivarair ākhyānam upajīvyate udayaprepsubhir bhṛtyair abhijāta iveśvaraḥ

3.1

kunəṅ(4) kottaman saṅ hyaṅ bhāratakathā, ri denyan sira nitya pinakopajīvana saṅ kavivara, kady aṅgan saṅ prabhu sujanmān pinakopajīvananiṅ vadva aṅusir(5) vibhava.

4.

itihāsottamād asmāj jāyante kavibuddhayaḥ | pañcabhya iva bhūtebhyo lokasaṁvidhayas trayaḥ || 4
Parallels
  • MBh01,002.237

4.1

apayāpan ikiṅ(6) aji bhāratakathā, saṅkaniṅ buddhi saṅ kavi, kady aṅganiṅ triloka an vijil saṅke pañcamahābhūta.

5.

anāśrityaitad ākhyānaṁ kathā bhuvi na vidyate | āhāram anupāśritya śarīrasyeva dhāraṇā || 5
Parallels
  • MBh01,002.240
    anāśrityaitad ākhyānaṃ kathā bhuvi na vidyate āhāram anapāśritya śarīrasyeva dhāraṇam

5.1

tātan hana aji riṅ bhuvana, tan pakāśraya ikiṅ(7) byāsavasana, kady aṅganiṅ śarīra tan hana, ya tan pakāśrayaṅ āhāra.

6.

śrutvā tv idam upākhyānaṁ śrāvyam anyan na rocate | puṁskokilarutaṁ śrutvā rūkṣā dhvāṁkṣasya vāg iva || 6
Parallels
  • MBh01,002.236

6.1

lavan vaneh kottamanira, yan hana sira tlas ruməṅə̄ rasaniki saṅ hyaṅ aji, pisaniṅu juga sira ahyuna ruməṅva kathāntara, tka riṅ gīta veṇu vīṇādi, kady aṅganiṅ vvaṅ ruməṅə̄ suśabdaniṅ kuvoṅ, huvus ruməsəp ri hati laṅə̄niṅ(8) svaranya, amaṅun harṣaniṅ citta, tan hana gantāni kahyuna(9) ruməṅva rəsniṅ śabdaniṅ gagak.

6.2

maṅkana liṅ bhagavān vararucin panamaskāra riṅ bhagavān byāsa, nəhər umujarakən kottamanikiṅ bhāratakathā, ikiṅ inaranan sārasamuccaya(10), sāra ṅaraniṅ viśeṣa, samuccaya(11) papupulnya, nahan mataṅnyan sārasamuccaya ṅaranikiṅ(12) saṅ hyaṅ aji, daməl bhagavān(13) vararuci, nihan pinkət bhagavān vaiśampāyana iṅ mahārāja janamejaya, i kālanira cumaritākən ikaṅ bhāratakathā, ya tiki vitaniṅ sārasamuccaya.

7.

dharme cārthe ca kāme ca mokṣe ca bharatarṣabha | yad ihāsti tad anyatra yan nehāsti na tat kvacit || 7
Parallels
  • MBh01,056.033 MBh18,005.038 The stanza appears in two places in the critical edition of the Mahābhārata, plus in two * passages (01,001.210d@003_0011 and 01,002.236d@005_0002), once with reading paramarṣabha.

7.1

anaku kamuṅ janamejaya, salvirniṅ vara-varah, yāvat makapadārthaṅ(14) caturvarga, sāvatāranya(15), sakopanyāsanya, hana juga ya ṅke, saṅkṣepanya, ikiṅ(16) hana ṅke, ya ika hana iṅ len saṅkeriki, ikaṅ tan hana ṅke, tan hana ika riṅ len(17) saṅkeriki.

8.

mānuṣaḥ sarvabhūteṣu vartate vai śubhāśubhe | aśubheṣu samāviṣṭaṁ śubheṣv evāvakārayet || 8
Parallels
  • MBh12,297.019
    mānasaṃ sarvabhūteṣu vartate vai śubhāśubhe aśubhebhyaḥ samākṣipya śubheṣv evāvatārayet

8.1

ri sakvehniṅ sarvabhūta, ikiṅ janma vvaṅ juga vnaṅ gumavayakən ikaṅ śubhāśubhakarma, kunəṅ yan əntasakna(18) riṅ śubhakarma juga ikaṅ aśubhakarma, phalaniṅ dadi vvaṅ.

9.

upabhogaiḥ parityaktaṁ nātmānam avasādayet | caṇḍālatve ’pi mānuṣyaṁ sarvathā tāta durlabham || 9
Parallels
  • MBh12.286.031
    upabhogair api tyaktaṃ nātmānam avasādayet caṇḍālatve ’pi mānuṣyaṃ sarvathā tāta durlabham

9.1

mataṅyan hayva juga vvaṅ manastāpa, an tan paribhava, si dadi vvaṅ ta pva kagə̄ṅakna(19) ri ambək, apayapan paramadurlabha ikiṅ si janma mānuṣa ṅaranya, yadyapi caṇḍālayoni tuvi.

10.

iyaṁ hi yoniḥ prathamā yāṁ prāpya jagatīpate | ātmānaṁ śakyate trātuṁ karmabhiḥ śubhalakṣaṇaiḥ || 10
Parallels
  • MBh12,286.032
    iyaṃ hi yoniḥ prathamā yāṃ prāpya jagatīpate ātmā vai śakyate trātuṃ karmabhiḥ śubhalakṣaṇaiḥ

10.1

apan ikiṅ dadi vvaṅ, uttama juga ya, nimittaniṅ maṅkana, vnaṅ vi ya tumuluṅ avaknya saṅkeṅ saṅsāra, makasādhanaṅ śubhakarma, hiṅaniṅ kottamaniṅ dadi vvaṅ ika.

11.

ihaiva narakavyādheś cikitsāṁ na karoti yaḥ | gatvā nirauṣadhaṁ sthānaṁ sarujaḥ kiṁ kariṣyati || 11
Parallels
  • GarP2,49.23 ihaiva narakavyādheścikitsāṃ na karoti yaḥ gatvā nirauṣadhaṃ deśaṃ vyādhitaḥ kiṃ kariṣyati
  • Mahasubhasitasamgraha6225 ihaiva narakavyādheś cikitsāṃ na karoti yaḥ gatvā nirauṣadhasthānaṃ sa rogī kiṃ kariṣyati
  • bhg4c_u The same stanza is cited by Madhusūdana ad Bhagavadgītā 16.20.

11.1

hana pva vvaṅ tan gavayakən ikaṅ śubhakarma, tambaniṅ narakaloka kāṅkən lara, pjah pva ya, vvaṅ alara mara riṅ deśa katunan tamba ta ṅaranika, rūpaniṅ tan katmu ikaṅ enak kolahanya.

12.

sopānabhūtaṁ svargasya mānuṣyaṁ prāpya durlabham | tathātmānaṁ samādadhyād dhvaṁseta na punar yathā || 12
Parallels
  • MBh12,309.079 sopānabhūtaṃ svargasya mānuṣyaṃ prāpya durlabham tathātmānaṃ samādadhyād bhraśyeta na punar yathā

12.1

paramārthanya, pəṅpə̄ṅən ta pva katəmvanikiṅ si dadi vvaṅ, durlabha vi ya ta, sākṣāt haṇḍaniṅ mara riṅ svarga ika, sanimittaniṅ tan tibā muvah ta pva damlakna.

13.

karmabhūmir iyaṁ brahman phalabhūmir asau matā | iha yat kurute karma tat paratropabhujyate || 13
Parallels
  • MBh03,245.018d*1176_01+03,245.019a MBh03,247.035

13.1

apan ikiṅ janma maṅke, pagavayan śubhāśubhakarma juga ya, ikaṅ ri pəna pabhuktyan karmaphala ika, kaliṅanya, ikaṅ śubhāśubhakarma maṅke, ri pəna ika an kabhukti phalanya, ri pgatni kabhuktyanya, maṅjanma ta ya muvah, tumūta vāsanāniṅ karmaphala, vāsanā ṅaraniṅ saṅskāra, turahniṅ ambə mātra, ya tinūtniṅ(20) paribhāṣā, svargacyuta, narakacyuta, kunaṅ ikaṅ śubhāśubhakarma ri pəna, tan paphala ika, mataṅnyan maṅke juga pəṅpə̄ṅa śubhāśubhakarma.

14.

mānuṣyaṁ durlabhaṁ prāpya vidyullasitacañcalam | bhavakṣaye matiḥ kāryā bhāvopakaraṇeṣu ca || 14
Parallels
  • Subhasitaratnakarandakatha002 mānuṣyaṃ durlabhaṃ prāpya vidyutsaṃpātacañcalam bhavakṣaye matiḥ kāryā bhavopakaraṇeṣu vā

14.1

ikiṅ taṅ janma vvaṅ, kṣaṇikasvabhāva ta ya, tan pahi lavan kḍapniṅ kilat, durlabha tovi, mataṅnyan pə̄ṅakna ya ri kagavayanniṅ dharmasādhana, sakāraṇaniṅ manāśanaṅ saṅsāra, svargaphala kunaṅ.

15.

yo durlabhataraṁ prāpya mānuṣyaṁ lobhato naraḥ | dharmāvamantā kāmātmā bhavet sakalavañcitaḥ || 15
Parallels
  • MBh12,286.034 yo durlabhataraṃ prāpya mānuṣyam iha vai naraḥ dharmāvamantā kāmātmā bhavet sa khalu vañcyate

15.1

hana pva tuməmuṅ dadi vvaṅ, vimukha riṅ dharmasādhana, jnək riṅ arthakāma ārah, lobhāmbəknya, ya ika kabañcana ṅaranya.

16.

mānuṣyaṁ mahāduṣprāpyaṁ taḍidvilasitopamam | tal labdhvā ya@di saṁsārān nāpakrāmati vañcitaḥ || 16
Parallels
  • unknown

16.1

ikaṅ maṅgih si dadi vvaṅ, prasiddha vvaṅ riṅ dharmasādhāna, tātan əntas saṅke saṅsāra, kabañcana ta ṅaranika.

17.

ūrdhvabāhur viraumy eṣa na ca kaś cic chr̥ṇoti me | dharmād arthaś ca kāmaś ca sa kim arthaṁ na sevyate || 17
Parallels
  • MBh18,005.049

17.1

nihan mata kami maṅke, manavai, maṅuvuh, mapitutur, liṅ mami, ikaṅ artha, kāma, malamakən dharma juga ṅulaha, hayva palaṅpaṅ lavan dharma maṅkana liṅ mami, ndātan hana juga aṅrəṅə̄ ri heturnyan evəh saṅ makolah dharmasādhana, apa kunaṅ hetunya.

18.

kāmārthau lipsamānas tu dharmam evāditaś caret | na hi dharmād apetyārthaḥ kāmo vāpi kadācana || 18
Parallels
  • MBh05,122.035

18.1

yan paramārthanya, yan arthakāma sādhyan, dharma juga ləkasakna rumuhun, niyata katəmvaniṅ arthakāma mne,(21) tan paramārtha vi katəmvaniṅ arthakāma, deniṅ anasar sakeṅ dharma.

19.

dhārmikaṁ pūjayanti ca na dhanāḍhyaṁ na kāminam | dhane sukhakalā kā cid dharme tu paramaṁ sukham || 19
Parallels
  • MBh12,263.054c MBh12,263.055a

19.1

kunaṅ saṅ paṇḍita, saṅ dhārmika juga, inastutinira, inaləmnira, an sira prasiddha anmu sukha, tan paṅaləm sugih, kāmī, apan tan tuhu sukha, ri hananiṅ ahaṅkārājñāna, ri sḍəṅniṅ dhanakāma vyavahāra.

20.

dharma eva plavo nānyaḥ svargaṁ samabhivāñchatām | sa ca naur vaṇijas taṭaṁ jaladheḥ pāram icchataḥ || 20
Parallels
  • MBh03,032.022

20.1

ikaṅ dharma ṅaranya, hnuniṅ mara riṅ svarga ika, kadi gatiniṅ parahu, an hnuniṅ baṇyāga nəntas iṅ tasik.

21.

yatnaḥ kāmārthamokṣāṇāṁ kr̥to ’pi hi vipadyate | dharmāya punar ārambhaḥ saṅkalpo ’pi na niṣphalaḥ || 21
Parallels
  • unknown

21.1

ikaṅ kayatnan ri kagavayaniṅ kāma, artha, mvaṅ mokṣa, dadi ika tan paphala, kunaṅ ikaṅ kayatnan riṅ dharmasādhana, niyata maphala ika, yadyapin aṅən-aṅənan juga, maphala atika.

22.

yathādityaḥ samudyan vai tamaḥ sarvaṁ vyapohati | evaṁ kalyāṇam ātiṣṭhan sarvapāpaṁ vyapohati || 22
Parallels
  • MBh03,198.053 MBh12,148.033

22.1

kadi krama saṅ hyaṅ āditya, an vijil, humilaṅakən ptəṅniṅ rāt, maṅkana tikaṅ vvaṅ mulahakən iṅ dharma, an hilaṅakən salviriṅ pāpa.

23.

yathā yathā hi puruṣaḥ kalyāṇe ramate manaḥ | tathā tathāsya siddhyanti sarvārthā nātra saṁśayaḥ || 23
Parallels
  • MBh05,035.034 MBh12,219.007

23.1

salviraniṅ vvaṅ kaniṣṭhamadhyamottama tuvi, yāvat gave hayu kajnəkni hatinya, niyata siddhaniṅ sasinādhyanya.

24.

dharmaḥ sadā hitaḥ puṁsāṁ dharmaś caivāśrayaḥ satām | dharmāl lokās trayas tāta pravr̥ttāḥ sacarācarāḥ || 24
Parallels
  • MBh12,297.006

24.1

mvaṅ kottaman ikaṅ dharma, prasiddha saṅkaniṅ hitāvasāna, irikaṅ mulahakən ya, mvaṅ pinakāśraya saṅ paṇḍita, saṅkṣepanya, dharma mantasakən ikaṅ triloka.

25.

yasya notkrāmati matir dharmamārgānusāriṇī | tam āhuḥ puṇyakarmāṇaṁ na śocyo mitrabāndhavaiḥ || 25
Parallels
  • MBh12,309.080

25.1

hana pva vvaṅ tan liṅgar apagəh buddhinya, ar tūtakən kadamlaniṅ dharmasādhana, ya ika vvaṅ bhāgyamanta liṅ saṅ paṇḍita, tan kalarākna deniṅ kadaṅ-mitranya, yadyan manāśakānapa-napa(22) maṅatīta jīvita tuvi.

26.

Vaṁśastha

yathekṣuhetor iha secitaṁ payaḥ tr̥ṇāni vallīr api samprasiñcati | tathā naro dharmapathena sañcaran yaśāṁsi kāmāni vasūni cāśnute || 26
Parallels
  • unknown

26.1

kunaṅ paramārthanya, kady aṅganiṅ vvai maṅəna tbu, tan ikaṅ tbu juga kānugrahan denika, milu tkaniṅ tr̥ṇalatādi, saparək ikaṅ tbu milu kānugrahan, maṅkana taṅ vvaṅ makapravr̥ttiṅ dharma, artha, kāma, yaśa kasambi denika.

27.

Vaṁśastha

surūpatām ātmaguṇaṁ ca vistaraṁ kulānvayaṁ dravyasamr̥ddhisaṁcayam | naro hi sarvvaṁ labhate yathākr̥taṁ sadā śubhenātmakr̥tena karmaṇā || 27
Parallels
  • MBh12,287.044

27.1

kunaṅ ikaṅ vvaṅ gumavay ikaṅ śubhakarma, janmanyan saṅke riṅ svargga dlāha, lituhayu maguṇa, sujanma, sugih, mavīrya, phalaniṅ śubhakarmāvasāna tinmunya.

28.

kāntāravanadurgeṣu kr̥cchreṣv āpatsu sambhrame | udyateṣu ca śastreṣu nāsti dharmavatāṁ bhayam || 28
Parallels
  • MBh05,039.053

28.1

lavan ta vaneh, riṅ hlət, riṅ alas, riṅ priṅga, riṅ laya, salvirniṅ duhkhahetu, ri papraṅan kunəṅ, tar tka juga ikaṅ bhaya, ri saṅ dhārmika, apan ikaṅ śubhakarma rumakṣa sira.

29.

manonukūlāḥ pramadā rūpavatyaḥ svalaṅkr̥tāḥ | vāsaḥ prāsādapr̥ṣṭhe ca bhavanti śubhakarmaṇām || 29
Parallels
  • MBh12,284.021

29.1

lavan ta vaneh, ikaṅ strīratna anakbi rahayu, saṅsaṅan riṅ sinaṇḍaṅ, vruh ri saṅinakana(23) riṅ jalu-jalu, lavan umah rahayu, makādi prāsādapr̥ṣṭha, upalakṣaṇa riṅ bhogopabhoga, mvaṅ anarghya(24) vastrābharaṇādi, dr̥bya saṅ puṇyakārī ika kabeh.

30.

nipānam iva maṇḍūkāḥ saraḥ pūrṇam ivāṇḍajāḥ | śubhakarmāṇam āyānt sahāyāś ca dhanāni ca || 30
Parallels
  • Hit_1.167 bib:Boehtlingk1872_01-3727/1585

30.1

apan ikaṅ balakośavāhana, tumkākən avaknya juga ya ri saṅ puṇyakarma, kadi kramaniṅ maṇḍūka, an parākna avaknya riṅ sumur, mvaṅ ikaṅ manuk, an tkākna avaknya riṅ talaga.

31.

nihan ulaha saṅ vaiśya, maṅajya sira ri saṅ brāhmaṇa, ri saṅ kṣatriya kunəṅ, mvaṅ maveha dāna ri tkaniṅ dānakāla, riṅ śubhadivasa, dum-dumananira ta sakvehniṅ mamarāśraya ri sira, magləma amūjā riṅ saṅ hyaṅ tryagni, saṅ hyaṅ tryagni ṅaranira saṅ hyaṅ apuy tiga, pratyekanira, āhavanīya, gārhaspatya, citāgni, āhavanīya ṅaranira apuyniṅ asuruhan, rumatəṅ i pinaṅan, gārhaspatya ṅaranira apuyniṅ vinaraṅ, apan agni sākṣikā kramaniṅ vinaraṅ i kālaniṅ vivāha, citāgni ṅaranira apuyniṅ manunu śava, nahan ta saṅ hyaṅ tryagni ṅaranira, sira ta pūjān de saṅ vaiśya, ulahnira ika maṅkana, ya tumkākən sira riṅ svarga dlāha.

66.

brahma kṣatraṁ vaiśyavarṇaṁ ca śūdraḥ krameṇaitān nyāyataḥ pūjyamānaḥ | tuṣṭeṣv eteṣv avyatho dagdhapāpas tyaktvā dehaṁ siddhim iṣṭāṁl labheta || 66
Parallels
  • MBh05,040.026

66.1

67.

rājā bhīrur brāhmaṇaḥ sarvabhakṣo vaiśyo ’nīhāvān hīnavarṇo ’lasaś ca | vidvān aśīlo vr̥ttahīnaḥ kulīnaḥ satyād bhraṣṭo brāhmaṇaḥ strī ca duṣṭā || 67
Parallels
  • MBh12,279.024

68.

69.

ārjavaṁ cānr̥śaṁsyaṁ ca damaś cendriyanigrahaḥ | eṣa sādhāraṇo dharmaś cāturvarṇye ’bravīn manuḥ || 69

71.

102.

anapa-napa = atapa-tapa? Neither form is attested in OJED. Raghu Vira’s critical apparatus (notes 8 and 9) suggests that at least one manuscript reads mānāśakānapamaṅatīta°, which could be used as support for an alternative emn (without reduplication) manāśakānapa maṅatīta° (with anapa = atapa). But a reduplicated form seems to be supported by the majority of witnesses, if this is what may be inferred from Raghu Vira’s negative apparatus.
